					QCQ = {is_puppet = no}
					has_war = no
					is_neighbor_of = QCQ
					QCQ = {has_war = yes}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = QCQ
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
					has_army_size = { size > 50 }
					QCQ = {is_in_faction = yes}
					has_war = no
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_neighbor_of = QCQ
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = QCQ
			}
		}
				###############################################################

					SKS = {is_puppet = no}

#AI Faction leaders
country_event = {
	id = ido.5
	title = ido.5.t
	desc = ido.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_molotov_ribentrop_handshake

	trigger = {
		threat > 0.5
		is_in_faction = no
		is_puppet = no
		is_ai = yes
		has_idea = home_of_the_free
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 50 }

	option = {
		name = ido.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
						AND = {
							any_neighbor_country = {
								has_government = democratic
								NOT = {is_in_faction = yes}
							}
							has_government = democratic
						}
				}
		}
			ROOT = {create_faction = "usastatesd"}
	}
	option = {
		name = ido.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
						AND = {
							any_neighbor_country = {
								has_government = communism
								NOT = {is_in_faction = yes}
							}
							has_government = communism
						}
				}
		}
			ROOT = {create_faction = "usastatesc"}
	}
	option = {
		name = ido.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
						AND = {
							any_neighbor_country = {
								has_government = fascism
								NOT = {is_in_faction = yes}
							}
							has_government = fascism
						}
				}
		}
			ROOT = {create_faction = "usastatesf"}
	}
}
